    var targetDefaultTracking = (function () {

        var _defaultMboxPrefix = "Target-Default";

        var _clickListenerSelectors = {}
        var _scrollListenerSelectors = {}
        var mBoxes = [];
        var _scrollsTracked = {}

        var _sendTrackingCall = function (mBoxes, optionalMboxSuffix, params, useCustomMboxPrefix) {
            for (var i = 0; i < mBoxes.length; i++) {
                var mbox = (useCustomMboxPrefix ? mBoxes[i] : _defaultMboxPrefix + '_' + mBoxes[i]) + (optionalMboxSuffix ? '_' + optionalMboxSuffix : '');
                adobe.target.trackEvent({
                    "mbox": mbox,
                    "params": params,
                    "timeout": 500
                });
                _satellite.logger.info("[TARGET] Tracking call sent - mbox= " + mbox + (params ? "; params=" + JSON.stringify(params) : ""));
            }
        }

        var _trackPercentScrolled = function () {

            var windowTop = window.pageYOffset;
            var windowBottom = windowTop + window.innerHeight;

            var scrollListeners = Object.keys(_scrollListenerSelectors);
            for (var i = 0; i < scrollListeners.length; i++) {
                var scrollListener = scrollListeners[i];
                if (!document.querySelector(scrollListener)) {
                    continue;
                }
                var container = document.querySelector(scrollListener);
                var containerTop = container.getBoundingClientRect().top + windowTop;
                var containerBottom = container.getBoundingClientRect().bottom + windowTop;
                var containerHeight = containerBottom - containerTop;

                var containerPercentScrolled = (windowBottom - containerTop) / containerHeight * 100;

                if (!_scrollsTracked[scrollListener]) {
                    _scrollsTracked[scrollListener] = [];
                }
                for (var j = 0; j < _scrollListenerSelectors[scrollListener].percentages.length; j++) {
                    var percentToTrack = _scrollListenerSelectors[scrollListener].percentages[j];
                    if (containerPercentScrolled >= percentToTrack && _scrollsTracked[scrollListener].indexOf(percentToTrack) == -1) {
                        _sendTrackingCall(_scrollListenerSelectors[scrollListener].mBox, percentToTrack.toString());
                        _scrollsTracked[scrollListener].push(percentToTrack);
                    }
                }
            }
        };

        var _addScrollEventListener = function () {
            var throttleScroll;
            window.addEventListener("scroll", function () {
                clearTimeout(throttleScroll);
                throttleScroll = setTimeout(function () {
                    _trackPercentScrolled();
                }, 200);
            });
        }

        var _addClickEventListener = function () {
            document.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                var selectors = Object.keys(_clickListenerSelectors);
                for (var i = 0; i < selectors.length; i++) {
                    if (e.target.closest(selectors[i])) {
                        _sendTrackingCall(_clickListenerSelectors[selectors[i]]);
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        var _getSelectorByMbox = function (mBox) {
            var clickSelectors = Object.keys(_clickListenerSelectors);
            for (var i = 0; i < clickSelectors.length; i++) {
                if (_clickListenerSelectors[clickSelectors[i]].indexOf(mBox) > -1) {
                    return clickSelectors[i] + " (Click)";
                }
            }

            var scrollSelectors = Object.keys(_scrollListenerSelectors);
            for (var i = 0; i < scrollSelectors.length; i++) {
                if (_scrollListenerSelectors[scrollSelectors[i]].mBox.indexOf(mBox) > -1) {
                    return scrollSelectors[i] + " (Scroll)";
                }
            }
        }

        return {

            addClickSelector: function (selector, mBox) {
                if (Object.keys(_clickListenerSelectors).length == 0) {
                    _addClickEventListener();
                }

                if (!_clickListenerSelectors[selector]) {
                    if (mBoxes.indexOf(mBox) == -1) {
                        _clickListenerSelectors[selector] = [mBox];
                        mBoxes.push(mBox);
                    } else {
                        _satellite.logger.error('[TARGET] Click-Selector "' + selector + '" not added because mBox "' + mBox + '" is used with different selector: ' + _getSelectorByMbox(mBox));
                    }
                } else {
                    if (_clickListenerSelectors[selector].indexOf(mBox) == -1) {
                        _clickListenerSelectors[selector].push(mBox);
                        mBoxes.push(mBox);
                        _satellite.logger.info('[TARGET] Click-Selector "' + selector + '" is used with different mBoxes: ' + _clickListenerSelectors[selector].toString());
                    }
                }
            },

            addScrollSelector: function (selector, mBox, percentages) {
                if (Object.keys(_scrollListenerSelectors).length == 0) {
                    _addScrollEventListener();
                }

                if (!_scrollListenerSelectors[selector]) {
                    if (mBoxes.indexOf(mBox) == -1) {
                        _scrollListenerSelectors[selector] = { "mBox": [mBox], "percentages": percentages };
                        mBoxes.push(mBox);
                    } else {
                        _satellite.logger.error('[TARGET] Scroll-Selector "' + selector + '" not added because mBox "' + mBox + '" is used with different selector: ' + _getSelectorByMbox(mBox));
                    }
                } else {
                    if (_scrollListenerSelectors[selector].mBox.indexOf(mBox) == -1) {
                        _scrollListenerSelectors[selector].mBox.push(mBox);
                        mBoxes.push(mBox);
                        _satellite.logger.info('[TARGET] Scroll-Selector "' + selector + '" is used with different mBoxes: ' + _scrollListenerSelectors[selector].mBox.toString());
                    }
                    for (var i = 0; i < percentages.length; i++) {
                        if (_scrollListenerSelectors[selector].percentages.indexOf(percentages[i]) == -1) {
                            _scrollListenerSelectors[selector].percentages.push(percentages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
            },

            sendTrackingCall: function (mBoxes, optionalMboxSuffix, params) {
                if (typeof mBoxes == "string") {
                    mBoxes = [mBoxes];
                }

                _sendTrackingCall(mBoxes, optionalMboxSuffix, params, true);
            }
        };
    })();
